<script>function getCookieValue(cookieName) {
  if (!cookieName || document.cookie.indexOf(cookieName) === -1) {
    return undefined;
  }

  try {
    var cookieArray = document.cookie.match(new RegExp("(^| )".concat(cookieName, "=([^;]+)")));

    if (cookieArray && cookieArray.length > 0) {
      return decodeURIComponent(cookieArray.pop());
    }

    return undefined;
  } catch (e) {
    return undefined;
  }
}; function getCustomerNameAndGreeting() {
  var isSignedIn = getCookieValue("hasCID") === "1";
  var customer = getCookieValue("customer");

  if (isSignedIn && customer && customer.length) {
    try {
      customer = JSON.parse(customer);

      if (customer.firstName) {
        return "Hi, ".concat(customer.firstName, " ").concat(customer.lastNameInitial);
      }

      return undefined;
    } catch (e) {
      return undefined;
    }
  }

  return undefined;
}; function replaceAccountSubLinkText() {
  var customerNameAndGreeting = getCustomerNameAndGreeting();
  var accountSubText = document.querySelector("#signIn");

  if (customerNameAndGreeting && accountSubText) {
    accountSubText.textContent = customerNameAndGreeting;
  }
};
    document.addEventListener("DOMContentLoaded", function () { 
      try{
        replaceAccountSubLinkText();
      } catch(e) {console.log("Error in glass-hf client code", e)}
    });
</script>

class="SEO-metadata" data-module="SEOCustomHTML" data-tl-id="tempo-module-SEOCustomHTML"><div><div class="collapsable classes has-toggle" id="Collapsable-1650916701858" style="min-height:160px"><div u-size-7-9-m u-size-6-10-xl"><span style="font-size:0"></span><div class="SeoCustomHtml" data-module="SEOText" data-module-id="categorypage-seoText" data-tl-id="categorypage-SEOCustomHTML"><div class="SeoCustomHtml-data"><h2>Motorcycle Parts &amp; Accessories</h2>
<p>There's more than one way to ride a motorcycle. Whether you're taking your sport or dirt bike to the track or going on an adventure with your cruiser or touring bike, Walmart.com has a wide variety of accessories and parts to suit your riding style at everyday low prices.</p>
<h3>What are some popular motorcycle accessories?</h3>
<p>
</p><ul><li><b>Motorcycle helmets:</b> A good helmet is an important accessory for riding your bike. A full-face, half, or open-face helmet can help protect your head and brain from injury in the event of an accident. Some helmets can also provide additional perks, such as Bluetooth capabilities, face shields, or visors and cheek pads for added protection. You can find a wide variety of modular helmets, dirt bike helmets, and dual sport helmets from brands like HJC, ICON, Sena, Bell Helmets, and Fuel Helmets. </li>
<li><b>Riding gear:</b> Riding jackets and pants can also help protect you from injuries and from the elements while you ride. Mesh and textile jackets and pants can help keep you cool when it's hot, while leather gear and gloves can keep you warm and dry in the rain. You can find a wide variety of motorcycle jackets, gloves, body armor, goggles and glasses, and boots from brands like Alpinestars, Joe Rocket, O'Neal Racing, Speed and Strength, and 100%. </li>
<li><b>Motorcycle tires:</b> For your safety, it's important to check your tires before every ride. If you can see the tread wear indicators, it's time to replace them. At Walmart, you can find a variety of motorcycle tires and replacement parts from brands like Goodyear, Bridgestone, and Continental.</li>
<b>Parts and accessories:</b> Whether it's Mobil1 motorcycle oil or cargo storage bags, you can find all the accessories you need to keep your motorcycle in tip-top shape. You can also find Bluetooth accessories and other electronics to get the most out of your ride, and motorcycle covers to help protect your bike when it's not in use.
</ul>
<p></p>
<p>From motorcycle batteries and jacks to riding jerseys and boots, you can find everything you need to get out and ride so you can save money and live better.</p></div></div></div></div></div></div><div class="SEO-metadata-bottom-fade"></div></div><div style="position:absolute;left:0;top:0;right:0;bottom:0;overflow:hidden;z-index:-1;visibility:hidden;pointer-events:none"><div style="position:absolute;left:0;top:0;right:0;bottom:0;overflow:hidden;z-index:-1;visibility:hidden;pointer-events:none"><div style="position:absolute;left:0;top:0;transition:0s;width:100000px;height:100000px"></div></div><div style="position:absolute;left:0;top:0;right:0;bottom:0;overflow:hidden;z-index:-1;visibility:hidden;pointer-events:none"><div style="position:absolute;left:0;top:0;transition:0s;width:200%;height:200%"></div></div></div></div></div><div class="revealer-footer text-center border"><button aria-controls="Collapsable-1650916701858" aria-expanded="false" aria-label="See More" class="button margin-bottom button--link" data-automation-id="button" data-tl-id="" type="button"><span class="button-wrapper">See more</span></button></div></div></div></div></div></div></div><div class="env-info ResponsiveContainer">Electrode, App-category-app, Comp-1353adf9-5c3a-4de8-bfdc-9cfdf4fefb43, DC-eus2-prod-a11, ENV-prod-a, PROF-PROD, VER-9.49.0, SHA-0824f913c02115e974cd2e0bc851e2f66aed0a9c, CID-</div></div></div></div>

<script>(function() {
  function getCookie(name) {
    if (name) {
      var cookieRegex = new RegExp(name + "=([^\\s;]*)");
      var sMatch = document.cookie.match(cookieRegex);
      if (sMatch && sMatch[1]) {
        return decodeURIComponent(sMatch[1]);
      }
    }
    return "";
  }

  function get(path, obj) {
    try {
      var val;
      var paths = typeof path === "string" ? path.split(".") : path;
      if (obj && typeof obj === "object") {
        paths.forEach(function(k, i) {
          if (i === 0) {
            val = obj[k];
          } else if (val) {
            val = val[k];
          }
        });
      }
      return val;
    } catch (e) {
      // In case of an error, prevents side effects on page level
      return;
    }
  }

  function getAppName() {
    return get("_wml.config.ui.applicationName", window);
  }

  function getMidasConfig() {
    return get("_wml.config.ccm.midasConfig", window) || {};
  }
  function getMidasUiConfig() {
    return get("_wml.config.ui.midasConfig", window) || {};
  }

  function getMidasCfgVal(cfgName) {
    var cfg = getMidasConfig();
    var appName = getAppName();
    var pageCfgKey = appName + "-" + cfgName;
    return cfg[pageCfgKey] || cfg[cfgName];
  }

  function loadScript(scriptUrl) {
    var script = document.createElement("script");
    script.async = true;
    script.src = scriptUrl;
    document.head.appendChild(script);
  }

  function loadAds() {
    if (!loadAds.loaded) {
      addPerfMark("load-midas-display");
      loadAds.loaded = true;
      var displayAds = getMidasCfgVal("displayAds") !== "false";
      if (displayAds) {
        var MDABT = getCookie("MDABT");
        var midasDisplayScript =
          getMidasCfgVal("test-" + MDABT) ||
          getMidasCfgVal("midasDisplayScript");
        var gptUrl = "//www.googletagservices.com/tag/js/gpt.js";
        if (getMidasCfgVal("loadDisplayScript") !== "false") {
          loadScript(midasDisplayScript);
        }
        loadScript(gptUrl);
      }
    }
  }

  function loadS2SScripts() {
    if (!loadS2SScripts.loaded) {
      addPerfMark("load-s2s-midas-scripts");
      loadS2SScripts.loaded = true;
      var MDABTS2S = getCookie("MDABTS2S");
      var midasS2SScript =
        getMidasCfgVal("test-" + MDABTS2S) || getMidasCfgVal("midasS2SScript");
      loadScript(midasS2SScript);
    }
  }

  function addPerfMark(markName){
    var hasPerfMark = !!get("performance.mark", window);
    if (hasPerfMark) {
      // For some reason it causes an error when you store the reference of the mark fn.
      window.performance.mark(markName);
    }
  }
  var loadS2SEvent =
    getCookie("loadS2SEvent") ||
    getMidasUiConfig()["loadS2SEvent"] ||
    getMidasCfgVal("loadS2SEvent") ||
    "hasS2SPayload";

  var loadEvent =
    getCookie("loadEvent") ||
    getMidasUiConfig()["loadEvent"] ||
    getMidasCfgVal("loadEvent") ||
    "instant";
  window._wml.adLoader = (function() {
    var eventListeners = {};
    return {
      fireEvent: function fireEvent(eventName) {
        addPerfMark('fire-event-' + eventName);
        var listeners = eventListeners[eventName];

        if (listeners) {
          listeners.forEach(function(listener) {
            listener();
          });
        }
      },
      subscribe: function subscribe(eventName, listener) {
        if (!eventListeners[eventName]) {
          eventListeners[eventName] = [];
        }

        eventListeners[eventName].push(listener);
      },
    };
  })();

  _wml.adLoader.subscribe(loadEvent, loadAds);
  _wml.adLoader.subscribe(loadS2SEvent, loadS2SScripts);
  _wml.adLoader.fireEvent("instant"); // Default load ads immediately
})();

var applicationName = _wml.config.ui.applicationName || "default";

var wpa = (
  _wml.config.ccm.midasConfig.wpa &&
  _wml.config.ccm.midasConfig.wpa !== "false"
);

var wpaForPageType = (
  _wml.config.ccm.midasConfig["wpa." + applicationName] &&
  _wml.config.ccm.midasConfig["wpa." + applicationName] !== "false"
);

if (wpa && wpaForPageType) {
  var midasScriptEl = document.createElement("script");
  midasScriptEl.src = _wml.config.ccm.midasConfig.midasScript;
  midasScriptEl.async = true;
  document.head.appendChild(midasScriptEl);
};</script>
